2.4.2 Page Titled (1 avvik)1 alvorlig
Testregel 2.4.2 (2.4.2 - Nivå AA)
SERIOUS

Page is missing h1 heading

<body class="hid1295 kommunemal templsetid9 pagelevel0 page469692 ppt469692 pagelogo frontpage pgn_hjem articlelisting hasnosubmenuitem widefull langno mojanuar AAAA">
Add a single h1 heading that describes the page content

Heading level skipped: h1 to h3

<a class="cp" href="https://www.custompublish.com/" target="_blank">Web levert av CustomPublish</a>
Add text like '(opens in new tab)' or use visually-hidden text for screen readers
